The O
Ayalon I-LOC
Cave I-LOC
is O
a O
large O
underground O
limestone O
cave O
located O
near O
Ramla I-LOC
, O
Israel I-LOC
. O

The O
cave O
, O
300 O
feet O
deep O
, O
with O

2.5 O

in O
Israel I-LOC
. O

Researchers O
announced O
that O
they O
have O
so O
far O
discovered O
eight O
new O
species O
, O
all O
without O

, O

four O

and O

. O

They O

two O

species O
and O

species O

that O
this O

region O
. O

The O
cave O

when O
a O

opening O
was O

. O

According O
to O

that O

. O

The O

to O

public O

. O

As O

was O

cut O

from O
the O
outside O
environment O

sustained O
an O
independent O

this O

did O
not O
rely O
on O
sunlight O
and O

, O
or O
on O
organic O
compounds O
, O
for O
an O
energy O
source O
. O

Rather O

was O
extracted O
by O

film O

pool O

. O

These O

in O

water O
, O
and O

air O
. O

These O

of O
the O
cave O
's O

. O
